<td valign="top"  style="width:30%;">
<p style="text-align:right;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:0pt;;text-indent:0pt;;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Exhibit 99.1</p></td>

</table></div>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:16pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-right:0.85%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:13pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-right:0.85%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:13pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-right:0.85%;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Mitek Reports Third Quarter Fiscal 2015 Financial Results </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-left:7.69%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:96.15%;margin-left:3.85%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Symbol';font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#183;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:96.15%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">Record quarterly revenue of $6.4 million, up 38% year-over-year</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:96.15%;margin-left:3.85%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Symbol';font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#183;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:96.15%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">Ten consecutive quarters of year-over-year revenue growth</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:96.15%;margin-left:3.85%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Symbol';font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#183;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:96.15%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">GAAP profit of $0.9 million, recording fourth consecutive profitable quarter</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:96.15%;margin-left:3.85%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Symbol';font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#183;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:96.15%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">Mobile Deposit<sup style="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&#174; </sup> surpasses new milestone, licensed by over 4,000 financial institutions</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:96.15%;margin-left:3.85%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.85%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:10pt;font-family:'Symbol';font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#183;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:96.15%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;">Acquired IDchecker, a global provider of identity document verification and facial recognition solutions </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">SAN DIEGO &#8211; July 23, 2015<font style="font-weight:normal;"> - Mitek Systems, Inc. (NASDAQ: MITK, </font><font style="color:#auto;text-decoration:underline;font-weight:normal;">www.miteksystems.com</font><font style="font-weight:normal;">), the leading innovator of mobile imaging for financial transactions and identification, today announced its financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2015, which ended June 30, 2015.&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#8220;Our quarterly revenue grew 38% year-over-year to over $6 million, demonstrating our success at providing a superior mobile experience,&#8221; said James B. DeBello, president and CEO of Mitek. &#8220;Our acquisition of IDchecker solidifies Mitek&#8217;s position as a global leader in mobile capture and identity solutions, increasing our recurring revenues with a cloud-based model.&#8221;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Total revenue for the third quarter of fiscal 2015 was $6.4 million compared to total revenue of $4.7 million in the third quarter of fiscal 2014, driven by Mitek&#8217;s Mobile Deposit<font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;"><sup style="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&#174;</sup></font> and identity solutions. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">GAAP net income for the third quarter of fiscal 2015 was $917,000, or $0.03 per diluted share, compared to GAAP net loss of $(1.6) million, or $(0.05) per share, in the third quarter of fiscal 2014. Non-GAAP net income for the third quarter of fiscal 2015 was $2.2 million, or $0.07 per diluted share, compared to non-GAAP net income of $139,000, or breakeven per diluted share, in the third quarter of fiscal 2014. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Fiscal 2015 Outlook</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Fiscal 2015 revenue is expected to be between $23.5 million to $24.5 million, an increase of $1 million to both ends of the prior guidance range.&nbsp;&nbsp; </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU2"></a><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Conference Call</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Mitek management will host a conference call and live webcast for analysts and investors today at 2 p.m. Pacific Time (5 p.m. Eastern Time) to discuss the Company's financial results. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">To listen to the live conference call, parties in the United States and Canada should dial 888-299-7209, access code 3912617. International parties should call 719-325-2308, access code 3912617.&nbsp;&nbsp;Please dial in approximately 10 minutes prior to the start of the call.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">A live and archived webcast of the conference call will be accessible on the "Investor Relations" section of the Company's website at www.miteksystems.com. To access the live webcast, please log in 10 minutes prior to the start of the call to download and install any necessary audio software. </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-right:3.85%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-right:3.85%;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">About Mitek&nbsp;&nbsp; </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-right:3.85%;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;">Headquartered in San Diego, CA, Mitek (NASDAQ: MITK) is the leading innovator of mobile capture and identity solutions for customer acquisition. Mitek&#8217;s mobile photo technology enables consumers to use the Camera as a Keyboard&#8482; to reduce friction for mobile check deposit, account opening, insurance quoting, payments, and ID document authentication. This innovative mobile technology is licensed by more than 4,100 organizations and used by tens of millions of consumers. In June of 2015, Mitek acquired IDchecker, a global provider of cloud based identity document verification and facial recognition solutions.&nbsp;&nbsp;The acquisition broadens Mitek&#8217;s global presence, expands document coverage to more than 3,500 document types and adds international customers in payments, financial services and information services. www.miteksystems.com MITK-F</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Notice Regarding Forward-Looking Statements </p>

Such forward-looking statements are subject to a number of risks and uncertainties, including, but not limited to, risks related to the Company&#8217;s ability to withstand negative conditions in the global economy, a lack of demand for or market acceptance of the Company&#8217;s products, the Company&#8217;s ability to continue to develop, produce and introduce innovative new products in a timely manner or the outcome of any pending or threatened litigation and the timing of the launch of Mobile Deposit</font><font style="letter-spacing:-0.2pt;"><sup style="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&#174;</sup></font><font style="Background-color:#FFFFFF;"> by the Company&#8217;s signed customers. </font></p>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Note Regarding Use of Non-GAAP Financial Measures</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">This news release contains non-GAAP financial measures for non-GAAP net income (loss) and non-GAAP net income (loss) per share that exclude stock compensation expenses, litigation costs, acquisition-related costs and expenses, and certain income tax provisions or benefits. These financial measures are not calculated in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) and are not based on any comprehensive set of accounting rules or principles. In evaluating the Company's performance, management uses certain non-GAAP financial measures to supplement financial statements prepared under GAAP. Management believes these non-GAAP financial measures provide a useful measure of the Company's operating results, a meaningful comparison with historical results and with the results of other companies, and insight into the Company's ongoing operating performance. Further, management and the Board of Directors utilize these non-GAAP financial measures to gain a better understanding of the Company's comparative operating performance from period-to-period and as a basis for planning and forecasting future periods. Management believes these non-GAAP financial measures, when read in conjunction with the Company's GAAP financials, are useful to investors because they provide a basis for meaningful period-to-period comparisons of the Company's ongoing operating results, including results of operations, against investor and analyst financial models, identifying trends in the Company's underlying business and performing related trend analyses, and they provide a better understanding of how management plans and measures the Company's underlying business.</p>
